while it is true spermatogenesis is a relatively long process, it is also a continuous process. it takes around 64 days for an immature cell to develop, while it travels from the basement membrane to the tubular lumen, which is when it reaches full maturity. only fully matured cells are released into the lumen. spermatogenesis is not a single event but a whole process. i'm not saying we should ejaculate. retaining seed is good, i support it 100.
**** *subreddit_semenretention *thread_hod39f *engajamento_alto

hey! this was my second mandala i ever drew so its incredibly easy. you'll need -drawing pad, no line paper or graph paper -a compass for making perfect circles -and a 12 inch clear ruler i watched youtube videos such as how to draw the flower of life and how to make a 32 ray mandala the only thing i did to create this was i made the flower of life, connected the intersections to form a star of david, sectioned that to make 2 triangles and used the 32 ray technique to build the outward designs. mine is 36 because i didnt really follow his exact thing i just understood the basics. if you dont want to waste paper and want to jump write in download the euclidia app on your phone. its an app that is built around geometry but theres tools in it that are so perfect for making beautiful designs like this and it takes only a minute compared to 3 days. much love stay safe

does masturbation reduce testosterone levels? the short answer is no, masturbation or indeed ejaculation in any form does not affect your male hormone to any significant extent. in fact, science has not produced conclusive evidence to show that there is a link between testosterone and masturbation at all. the short answer to this question? no. masturbation and ejaculation havent been shown to have any long-term or negative effects on testosterone levels, also known as t levels. ejaculation results in changes in prolactin increase and dopamine temporary decrease, but does not result in changes in testosterone. although prolactin and dopamine are both involved with testosterone, they do not appear to influence testosterone levels acutely. masturbation does not seem to have any long-lasting effects on testosterone levels. however, masturbation may have short-term effects on the levels of this hormone. it also affects other factors, such as sex drive. have more sex. ironically, although testosterone deficiency can cause problems with sexual desire and performance, having sex can actually increase your testosterone production. if you are having sex very infrequently this is likely to reduce your testosterone levels.
